 (ambala se kamalprit sabarwal or rohtak se surendra singh ke input ke saath) In Chhajarasi village, phase-iii area of noida, a person was slit with a sharp-edged weapon on Monday night
 mritak kii pahchaan murari jatav ke rup main hui he
 Murari Jatav, originally from Khurja, Bulandshahar, was living alone here
